FileWatcher stop working if the FileWatcher object is collected by GC
The `FileWatcher` will stop working if the FileWatcher object is collected by GC, it should keep process running and only be cleaned up when `FW.close()` is called, just like `tjs.serve`.
```ts
// define a variable to hold a reference of FileWatcher object
const h = tjs.watch("./test.txt", () => {
	console.log("works");
})

tjs.watch("./test.txt", () => {
	console.log("disposed");
})

// Process will exit if there is only a FileWatcher is running, use a infinite promise to keep process running
await new Promise(res => {});
```


</pr_description>

    31	    uv_fs_event_t handle;

    35	} TJSFsWatch;

    38	
    39	static TJSFsWatch *tjs_fswatch_get(JSValue obj) {
    40	    return JS_GetOpaque(obj, tjs_fswatch_class_id);
    41	}
    42	
    43	static void uv__fsevent_close_cb(uv_handle_t *handle) {
    44	    TJSFsWatch *fw = handle->data;
    45	    if (fw) {
    46	        fw->closed = 1;
    47	        if (fw->finalized) {
    48	            tjs__free(fw);
    49	        }
    50	    }
    51	}
    52	
    53	static void maybe_close(TJSFsWatch *fw) {
    54	    if (!uv_is_closing((uv_handle_t *) &fw->handle)) {
    55	        uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &fw->handle, uv__fsevent_close_cb);
    56	    }
    57	}
    58	
    59	static void tjs_fswatch_finalizer(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val) {
    60	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(val);
    61	    if (fw) {
    62	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, fw->callback);
    63	        fw->finalized = 1;
    64	        if (fw->closed) {
    65	            tjs__free(fw);
    66	        } else {
    67	            maybe_close(fw);
    68	        }
    69	    }
    70	}
    71	
    72	static void tjs_fswatch_mark(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val, JS_MarkFunc *mark_func) {
    73	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(val);
    74	    if (fw) {
    75	        JS_MarkValue(rt, fw->callback, mark_func);
    76	    }
    77	}

    85	static JSValue tjs_fswatch_close(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    86	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(this_val);
    87	    if (!fw) {
    88	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    89	    }

    91	    return JS_UNDEFINED;

    95	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(this_val);
    96	    if (!fw) {
    97	        return JS_UNDEFINED;
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    char buf[1024];
   101	    size_t size = sizeof(buf);
   102	    char *dbuf = buf;
   103	    int r;
   104	
   105	    r = uv_fs_event_getpath(&fw->handle, dbuf, &size);
   106	    if (r != 0) {
   107	        if (r != UV_ENOBUFS) {
   108	            return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   109	        }
   110	        dbuf = js_malloc(ctx, size);
   111	        if (!dbuf) {
   112	            return JS_EXCEPTION;
   113	        }
   114	        uv_fs_event_getpath(&fw->handle, dbuf, &size);
   115	        if (r != 0) {
   116	            js_free(ctx, dbuf);
   117	            return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   118	        }
   119	    }
   120	
   121	    JSValue ret = JS_NewStringLen(ctx, dbuf, size);
   122	
   123	    if (dbuf != buf) {
   124	        js_free(ctx, dbuf);
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    return ret;
   128	}

   130	static void uv__fs_event_cb(uv_fs_event_t *handle, const char *filename, int events, int status) {
   131	    TJSFsWatch *fw = handle->data;
   132	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(fw);
   133	    JSContext *ctx = fw->ctx;
   134	
   135	    // TODO: handle error case?
   136	    if (status != 0) {
   137	        return;
   138	    }
   139	
   140	    // libuv could set both, if we get rename, ignore change.
   141	
   142	    JSValue event;
   143	    if (events & UV_RENAME) {
   144	        event = JS_NewString(ctx, "rename");
   145	    } else if (events & UV_CHANGE) {
   146	        event = JS_NewString(ctx, "change");
   147	    } else {
   148	        // This shouldn't happen.
   149	        CHECK(0 && "invalid fs events");
   150	        return;
   151	    }
   152	
   153	    JSValue args[2] = {
   154	        JS_NewString(ctx, filename),
   155	        event,
   156	    };
   157	
   158	    tjs_call_handler(ctx, fw->callback, countof(args), args);
   159	
   160	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, args[0]);
   161	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, args[1]);
   162	}
   163	
   164	static JSValue tjs_fs_watch(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
   165	    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
   166	    if (!path) {
   167	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    if (!JS_IsFunction(ctx, argv[1])) {
   171	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   172	        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "no callback function provided");
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    JSValue obj = JS_NewObjectClass(ctx, tjs_fswatch_class_id);
   176	    if (JS_IsException(obj)) {
   177	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   178	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
   179	    }
   180	
   181	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs__mallocz(sizeof(*fw));
   182	    if (!fw) {
   183	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   184	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   185	        return JS_ThrowOutOfMemory(ctx);
   186	    }
   187	
   188	    int r = uv_fs_event_init(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fw->handle);
   189	    if (r != 0) {
   190	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   191	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   192	        tjs__free(fw);
   193	        return JS_ThrowInternalError(ctx, "couldn't initialize handle");
   194	    }
   195	
   196	    r = uv_fs_event_start(&fw->handle, uv__fs_event_cb, path, UV_FS_EVENT_RECURSIVE);
   197	    if (r != 0) {
   198	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   199	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   200	        tjs__free(fw);
   201	        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   202	    }
   203	
   204	    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   205	
   206	    fw->ctx = ctx;
   207	    fw->handle.data = fw;
   208	    fw->callback = JS_DupValue(ctx, argv[1]);
   209	
   210	    JS_SetOpaque(obj, fw);
   211	    return obj;
   212	}

   232	
   233	    JS_SetPropertyFunctionList(ctx, ns, tjs_fswatch_funcs, countof(tjs_fswatch_funcs));
   234	}

    33	#ifndef MIN
    34	#define MIN(a, b) ((a) < (b) ? (a) : (b))

    37	/*
    38	 * Pending write for streaming responses (modeled after TJSWsPendingWrite in ws.c).
    39	 */
    40	typedef struct {
    41	    struct list_head link;
    42	    uint8_t *data; /* includes LWS_PRE padding before actual data */
    43	    size_t len;    /* length of actual data (not including LWS_PRE) */
    44	    bool is_final;
    45	} TJSHttpPendingWrite;
    46	
    47	/*
    48	 * Per-request state, managed by us (not by lws per_session_data_size).
    49	 */
    50	typedef struct TJSHttpRequest {
    51	    UT_hash_handle hh;
    52	    struct lws *wsi;
    53	    uint64_t id;
    54	
    55	    /* Request data accumulated during callbacks. */
    56	    JSValue headers_arr; /* flat JS array: [name, value, name, value, ...] */
    57	    TBuf body_buf;
    58	    int method;
    59	    char url[2048];
    60	    char remote_addr[64];
    61	    bool body_complete;
    62	    bool chunked; /* true for Transfer-Encoding: chunked — body is streamed to JS */
    63	
    64	    /* Response state. */
    65	    bool responded;
    66	    bool streaming;
    67	    struct list_head pending_writes;
    68	    uint8_t *response_data; /* includes LWS_PRE padding */
    69	    size_t response_len;    /* total length including LWS_PRE + headers + body */
    70	    size_t response_offset; /* current send offset (relative to start of headers, i.e. LWS_PRE) */
    71	    size_t header_len;      /* length of headers portion */
    72	} TJSHttpRequest;
    73	
    74	/*
    75	 * Pending write for WS server connections.
    76	 */
    77	typedef struct {
    78	    struct list_head link;
    79	    uint8_t *data;
    80	    size_t len;
    81	    bool is_text;
    82	} TJSWsServerPendingWrite;
    83	
    84	/*
    85	 * Per-WS-connection state (allocated when server.upgrade() is called).
    86	 */
    87	typedef struct TJSWsConnection {
    88	    JSContext *ctx;
    89	    JSValue this_val; /* prevent GC (the JS ws object) */
    90	    JSValue data;     /* ws.data (user-provided per-connection state) */
    91	    struct lws *wsi;
    92	    UT_hash_handle hh; /* for pending_upgrades hash table (keyed by wsi) */
    93	    TBuf recv_buf;
    94	    bool recv_is_binary;
    95	    struct list_head pending_writes;
    96	    uint16_t close_code;
    97	    char close_reason[124];
    98	    char remote_addr[64];
    99	    /* Custom response headers for the 101 upgrade (parallel arrays, consumed in ADD_HEADERS). */
   100	    JSValue header_names;
   101	    JSValue header_values;
   102	} TJSWsConnection;
   103	
   104	enum { WS_EVENT_OPEN = 0, WS_EVENT_MESSAGE, WS_EVENT_CLOSE, WS_EVENT_ERROR, WS_EVENT_MAX };
   105	
   106	/*
   107	 * Per-upgrade context, lives from HTTP_CONFIRM_UPGRADE until _acceptUpgrade
   108	 * consumes it (or until the end of the synchronous JS call if not consumed).
   109	 */
   110	typedef struct {
   111	    uint64_t id;
   112	    struct lws *wsi;
   113	    UT_hash_handle hh;
   114	    char remote_addr[64];
   115	} TJSUpgradeCtx;
   116	
   117	/*
   118	 * Per-server state.
   119	 */
   120	typedef struct {
   121	    JSContext *ctx;
   122	    JSValue callback;                   /* JS onrequest handler */
   123	    JSValue body_chunk_callback;        /* JS onBodyChunk handler for streaming bodies */
   124	    JSValue this_val;                   /* prevent GC while listening */
   125	    JSValue ws_callbacks[WS_EVENT_MAX]; /* server-level: open, message, close, error */
   126	    struct lws_vhost *vhost;
   127	    int port;
   128	    bool closed;
   129	    uint64_t next_req_id;
   130	    uint64_t next_upgrade_id;
   131	    TJSHttpRequest *active_requests;   /* uthash table keyed by id */
   132	    TJSUpgradeCtx *upgrade_contexts;   /* uthash table keyed by id */
   133	    TJSWsConnection *pending_upgrades; /* uthash table keyed by wsi */
   134	    /* Mutable protocol name buffer.  During a WS upgrade the name is
   135	     * temporarily swapped to the negotiated subprotocol so that lws's own
   136	     * protocol matching and Sec-WebSocket-Protocol response header work
   137	     * correctly.  Reset in LWS_CALLBACK_ESTABLISHED / rejection. */
   138	    char ws_protocol_name[256];
   139	    /* TLS data, kept alive for the lifetime of the vhost. */
   140	    char *ssl_cert_mem;
   141	    char *ssl_key_mem;
   142	    char *ssl_ca_mem;
   143	    char *ssl_passphrase;
   144	} TJSHttpServer;
   145	
   146	static JSClassID tjs_httpserver_class_id;
   147	static JSClassID tjs_wsconn_class_id;
   148	
   149	static void tjs_http_req_free(JSRuntime *rt, TJSHttpRequest *req) {
   150	    if (!req) {
   151	        return;
   152	    }
   153	    JS_FreeValueRT(rt, req->headers_arr);
   154	    tbuf_free(&req->body_buf);
   155	    js_free_rt(rt, req->response_data);
   156	
   157	    /* Free any pending streaming writes. */
   158	    struct list_head *el, *el1;
   159	    list_for_each_safe(el, el1, &req->pending_writes) {
   160	        TJSHttpPendingWrite *pw = list_entry(el, TJSHttpPendingWrite, link);
   161	        list_del(&pw->link);
   162	        js_free_rt(rt, pw->data);
   163	        js_free_rt(rt, pw);
   164	    }
   165	
   166	    js_free_rt(rt, req);
   167	}
   168	
   169	static void tjs_wsconn_finalizer(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val) {
   170	    TJSWsConnection *ws = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_wsconn_class_id);
   171	    if (ws) {
   172	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, ws->data);
   173	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, ws->header_names);
   174	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, ws->header_values);
   175	
   176	        struct list_head *el, *el1;
   177	        list_for_each_safe(el, el1, &ws->pending_writes) {
   178	            TJSWsServerPendingWrite *pw = list_entry(el, TJSWsServerPendingWrite, link);
   179	            list_del(&pw->link);
   180	            js_free_rt(rt, pw->data);
   181	            js_free_rt(rt, pw);
   182	        }
   183	
   184	        tbuf_free(&ws->recv_buf);
   185	        js_free_rt(rt, ws);
   186	    }
   187	}
   188	
   189	static void tjs_wsconn_mark(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val, JS_MarkFunc *mark_func) {
   190	    TJSWsConnection *ws = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_wsconn_class_id);
   191	    if (ws) {
   192	        JS_MarkValue(rt, ws->data, mark_func);
   193	        JS_MarkValue(rt, ws->header_names, mark_func);
   194	        JS_MarkValue(rt, ws->header_values, mark_func);
   195	    }
   196	}
   197	
   198	static JSClassDef tjs_wsconn_class = {
   199	    "WsConnection",
   200	    .finalizer = tjs_wsconn_finalizer,
   201	    .gc_mark = tjs_wsconn_mark,
   202	};
   203	
   204	static TJSWsConnection *tjs_wsconn_get(JSContext *ctx, JSValue obj) {
   205	    return JS_GetOpaque2(ctx, obj, tjs_wsconn_class_id);
   206	}
   207	
   208	static void tjs_httpserver_finalizer(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val) {
   209	    TJSHttpServer *s = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_httpserver_class_id);
   210	    if (s) {
   211	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->callback);
   212	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->body_chunk_callback);
   213	
   214	        for (int i = 0; i < WS_EVENT_MAX; i++) {
   215	            JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->ws_callbacks[i]);
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        TJSHttpRequest *req, *tmp;
   219	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->active_requests, req, tmp) {
   220	            HASH_DEL(s->active_requests, req);
   221	            tjs_http_req_free(rt, req);
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        /* Release any unconsumed upgrade contexts. */
   225	        TJSUpgradeCtx *uctx, *uctx_tmp;
   226	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->upgrade_contexts, uctx, uctx_tmp) {
   227	            HASH_DEL(s->upgrade_contexts, uctx);
   228	            js_free_rt(rt, uctx);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        /* Release any pending WS upgrades that never completed. */
   232	        TJSWsConnection *ws, *ws_tmp;
   233	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->pending_upgrades, ws, ws_tmp) {
   234	            HASH_DEL(s->pending_upgrades, ws);
   235	            JSValue cls_val = ws->this_val;
   236	            ws->this_val = JS_UNDEFINED;
   237	            JS_FreeValueRT(rt, cls_val);
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_cert_mem);
   241	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_key_mem);
   242	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_ca_mem);
   243	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_passphrase);
   244	
   245	        js_free_rt(rt, s);
   246	    }
   247	}
   248	
   249	static void tjs_httpserver_mark(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val, JS_MarkFunc *mark_func) {
   250	    TJSHttpServer *s = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_httpserver_class_id);
   251	    if (s) {
   252	        JS_MarkValue(rt, s->callback, mark_func);
   253	        JS_MarkValue(rt, s->body_chunk_callback, mark_func);
   254	        for (int i = 0; i < WS_EVENT_MAX; i++) {
   255	            JS_MarkValue(rt, s->ws_callbacks[i], mark_func);
   256	        }
   257	    }
   258	}
   259	
   260	static JSClassDef tjs_httpserver_class = {
   261	    "HttpServer",
   262	    .finalizer = tjs_httpserver_finalizer,
   263	    .gc_mark = tjs_httpserver_mark,
   264	};
   265	
   266	static TJSHttpServer *tjs_httpserver_get(JSContext *ctx, JSValue obj) {
   267	    return JS_GetOpaque2(ctx, obj, tjs_httpserver_class_id);
   268	}
   269	
   270	typedef struct {
   271	    JSContext *ctx;
   272	    struct lws *wsi;
   273	    JSValue arr;
   274	    uint32_t idx;
   275	} TJSHeaderCollectCtx;
   276	
   277	static void tjs_http_custom_header_cb(const char *name, int nlen, void *opaque) {
   278	    TJSHeaderCollectCtx *hctx = (TJSHeaderCollectCtx *) opaque;
   279	
   280	    int total_len = lws_hdr_custom_length(hctx->wsi, name, nlen);
   281	    if (total_len < 0) {
   282	        return;
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    size_t buf_size = (size_t) total_len + 1;
   286	    char *val = js_malloc(hctx->ctx, buf_size);
   287	    if (!val) {
   288	        return;
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    int vlen = lws_hdr_custom_copy(hctx->wsi, val, (int) buf_size, name, nlen);
   292	    if (vlen >= 0) {
   293	        /* name includes trailing ':', strip it. */
   294	        int name_len = nlen;
   295	        if (name_len > 0 && name[name_len - 1] == ':') {
   296	            name_len--;
   297	        }
   298	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(hctx->ctx, hctx->arr, hctx->idx++, JS_NewStringLen(hctx->ctx, name, name_len));
   299	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(hctx->ctx, hctx->arr, hctx->idx++, JS_NewStringLen(hctx->ctx, val, vlen));
   300	    }
   301	
   302	    js_free(hctx->ctx, val);
   303	}
   304	
   305	static JSValue tjs_http_collect_headers(JSContext *ctx, struct lws *wsi) {
   306	    JSValue arr = JS_NewArray(ctx);
   307	    uint32_t idx = 0;
   308	
   309	    /* Collect well-known headers via lws token iteration. */
   310	    for (int n = 0; n < WSI_TOKEN_COUNT; n++) {
   311	        const unsigned char *tok_name = lws_token_to_string(n);
   312	        if (!tok_name) {
   313	            continue;
   314	        }
   315	        const char *tn = (const char *) tok_name;
   316	        int tn_len = (int) strlen(tn);
   317	        if (tn_len == 0 || tn[tn_len - 1] != ':') {
   318	            continue;
   319	        }
   320	        int total_len = lws_hdr_total_length(wsi, n);
   321	        if (total_len <= 0) {
   322	            continue;
   323	        }
   324	        size_t buf_size = (size_t) total_len + 1;
   325	        char *val = js_malloc(ctx, buf_size);
   326	        if (!val) {
   327	            continue;
   328	        }
   329	        if (lws_hdr_copy(wsi, val, (int) buf_size, n) < 0) {
   330	            js_free(ctx, val);
   331	            continue;
   332	        }
   333	        /* Strip trailing colon from token name. */
   334	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(ctx, arr, idx++, JS_NewStringLen(ctx, tn, tn_len - 1));
   335	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(ctx, arr, idx++, JS_NewString(ctx, val));
   336	        js_free(ctx, val);
   337	    }
   338	
   339	    /* Collect custom (unknown) headers. */
   340	    TJSHeaderCollectCtx hctx = { .ctx = ctx, .wsi = wsi, .arr = arr, .idx = idx };
   341	    lws_hdr_custom_name_foreach(wsi, tjs_http_custom_header_cb, &hctx);
   342	    return arr;
   343	}
   344	
   345	static const char *tjs_http_method_name(int method_idx) {
   346	    /* clang-format off */
   347	    static const char *method_names[] = {
   348	        [LWSHUMETH_GET] = "GET",
   349	        [LWSHUMETH_POST] = "POST",
   350	        [LWSHUMETH_OPTIONS] = "OPTIONS",
   351	        [LWSHUMETH_PUT] = "PUT",
   352	        [LWSHUMETH_PATCH] = "PATCH",
   353	        [LWSHUMETH_DELETE] = "DELETE",
   354	        [LWSHUMETH_CONNECT] = "CONNECT",
   355	        [LWSHUMETH_HEAD] = "HEAD",
   356	    };
   357	    /* clang-format on */
   358	
   359	    if (method_idx >= 0 && method_idx < (int) countof(method_names)) {
   360	        return method_names[method_idx];
   361	    }
   362	
   363	    return "GET";
   364	}
   365	
   366	/*
   367	 * Invoke the JS onrequest callback with request data.
   368	 */
   369	static void tjs_http_invoke_handler(TJSHttpServer *s, TJSHttpRequest *req) {
   370	    JSContext *ctx = s->ctx;
   371	
   372	    JSValue args[8];
   373	    args[0] = JS_NewInt64(ctx, req->id);
   374	    args[1] = JS_NewString(ctx, tjs_http_method_name(req->method));
   375	    args[2] = JS_NewString(ctx, req->url);
   376	    args[3] = JS_DupValue(ctx, req->headers_arr);
   377	    if (req->body_buf.size > 0) {
   378	        args[4] = JS_NewArrayBufferCopy(ctx, req->body_buf.buf, req->body_buf.size);
   379	    } else {
   380	        args[4] = JS_NULL;
   381	    }
   382	    args[5] = JS_NewString(ctx, req->remote_addr);
   383	    args[6] = JS_FALSE; /* not a WS upgrade */
   384	    args[7] = JS_NewBool(ctx, req->chunked);
   385	
   386	    tjs_call_handler(ctx, s->callback, countof(args), args);
   387	
   388	    for (size_t i = 0; i < countof(args); i++) {
   389	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, args[i]);
   390	    }
   391	}
   392	
   393	/*
   394	 * LWS HTTP server callback.
   395	 *
   396	 * Handles both HTTP requests and WebSocket connections (after upgrade).
   397	 * We use lws_set_wsi_user / lws_wsi_user to associate per-connection data
   398	 * (TJSHttpRequest or TJSWsConnection) with each wsi.
   399	 * After upgrade, lws rebinds to protocol[0] (this callback) so WS reason
   400	 * codes (ESTABLISHED, RECEIVE, SERVER_WRITEABLE, CLOSED) fire here.
   401	 */
   402	static int tjs_http_callback(struct lws *wsi, enum lws_callback_reasons reason, void *user, void *in, size_t len) {
   403	    /* Get the server from the vhost user pointer. */
   404	    TJSHttpServer *s = NULL;
   405	    struct lws_vhost *vh = lws_get_vhost(wsi);
   406	    if (vh) {
   407	        s = (TJSHttpServer *) lws_get_vhost_user(vh);
   408	    }
   409	
   410	    /* If the server is gone, reject everything. */
   411	    if (!s) {
   412	        return 0;
   413	    }
   414	
   415	
   416	    /* If the server is closed, still allow cleanup callbacks through. */
   417	    if (s->closed) {
   418	        switch (reason) {
   419	            case LWS_CALLBACK_WS_PEER_INITIATED_CLOSE:
   420	            case LWS_CALLBACK_CLOSED:
   421	            case LWS_CALLBACK_CLOSED_HTTP:
   422	            case LWS_CALLBACK_PROTOCOL_DESTROY:
   423	                break;
   424	            default:
   425	                return 0;
   426	        }
   427	    }
   428	
   429	    switch (reason) {
   430	        /*
   431	         * WebSocket callbacks (after upgrade).
   432	         */
   433	        case LWS_CALLBACK_ADD_HEADERS: {
   434	            /* Add custom headers to the 101 upgrade response. */
   435	            TJSWsConnection *ws = NULL;
   436	            HASH_FIND_PTR(s->pending_upgrades, &wsi, ws);
   437	            if (!ws || !JS_IsArray(ws->header_names)) {
   438	                break;
   439	            }
   440	
   441	            struct lws_process_html_args *args = (struct lws_process_html_args *) in;
   442	            unsigned char **p = (unsigned char **) &args->p;
   443	            unsigned char *end = (unsigned char *) args->p + args->max_len;
   444	            JSContext *ctx = ws->ctx;
   445	            int64_t n_headers;
   446	            JS_GetLength(ctx, ws->header_names, &n_headers);
   447	
   448	            for (int64_t i = 0; i < n_headers; i++) {
   449	                JSValue js_name = JS_GetPropertyUint32(ctx, ws->header_names, i);
   450	                JSValue js_value = JS_GetPropertyUint32(ctx, ws->header_values, i);
   451	
   452	                const char *name = JS_ToCString(ctx, js_name);
   453	                const char *value = JS_ToCString(ctx, js_value);
   454	                JS_FreeValue(ctx, js_name);
   455	                JS_FreeValue(ctx, js_value);
   456	
   457	                if (!name || !value) {
   458	                    JS_FreeCString(ctx, name);
   459	                    JS_FreeCString(ctx, value);
   460	                    return -1;
   461	                }
   462	
   463	                /* Skip sec-websocket-protocol — handled via lws protocol name. */
   464	                if (!strcasecmp(name, "sec-websocket-protocol:")) {
   465	                    JS_FreeCString(ctx, name);
   466	                    JS_FreeCString(ctx, value);
   467	                    continue;
   468	                }
   469	
   470	                int r = lws_add_http_header_by_name(wsi,
   471	                                                    (const unsigned char *) name,
   472	                                                    (const unsigned char *) value,
   473	                                                    (int) strlen(value),

    93	    return sab->buf;
    94	}
    95	
    96	void tjs__sab_free(void *opaque, void *ptr) {
    97	    TJSSABHeader *sab = (TJSSABHeader *) ((uint8_t *) ptr - sizeof(TJSSABHeader));
    98	    int ref_count = atomic_add_int(&sab->ref_count, -1);
    99	    assert(ref_count >= 0);
   100	    if (ref_count == 0) {
   101	        tjs__free(sab);
   102	    }
   103	}
   104	
   105	void tjs__sab_dup(void *opaque, void *ptr) {
   106	    TJSSABHeader *sab = (TJSSABHeader *) ((uint8_t *) ptr - sizeof(TJSSABHeader));
   107	    atomic_add_int(&sab->ref_count, 1);
   108	}
   109	
   110	static const JSSharedArrayBufferFunctions tjs_sf = {
   111	    .sab_alloc = tjs__sab_alloc,
   112	    .sab_dup = tjs__sab_dup,
   113	    .sab_free = tjs__sab_free,
   114	    .sab_opaque = NULL,
   115	};

   130	static JSValue tjs__set_cookie_jar_path(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
   131	    TJSRuntime *qrt = TJS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   132	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   133	
   134	    CHECK_EQ(qrt->lws.cookie_jar_path, NULL);
   135	
   136	    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
   137	    if (!path) {
   138	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    qrt->lws.cookie_jar_path = js_strdup(ctx, path);
   142	    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   143	
   144	    return JS_UNDEFINED;
   145	}

   147	static JSValue tjs__set_ca_bundle_path(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
   148	    TJSRuntime *qrt = TJS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   149	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   150	
   151	    CHECK_EQ(qrt->lws.ca_bundle_path, NULL);
   152

   163	
   164	static JSValue tjs__js_drain_microtasks(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
   165	    TJSRuntime *qrt = TJS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   166	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   167	
   168	    /* Re-entrancy guard: mirrors the HTML spec's "performing a microtask
   169	     * checkpoint" flag.  Without this, draining microtasks inside
   170	     * dispatchEvent can cause unbounded nesting of JS_ExecutePendingJob
   171	     * when a microtask dispatches another event. */
   172	    if (qrt->draining_microtasks) {
   173	        return JS_UNDEFINED;
   174	    }
   175	
   176	    qrt->draining_microtasks = true;
   177	    tjs__drain_microtasks(ctx);
   178	    qrt->draining_microtasks = false;
   179	
   180	    return JS_UNDEFINED;
   181	}

   183	static void tjs__bootstrap_core(JSContext *ctx, JSValue ns) {
   184	    tjs__mod_dns_init(ctx, ns);
   185	    tjs__mod_engine_init(ctx, ns);
   186	    tjs__mod_error_init(ctx, ns);
   187	    tjs__mod_ffi_init(ctx, ns);
   188	    tjs__mod_fs_init(ctx, ns);
   189	    tjs__mod_fswatch_init(ctx, ns);
   190	    tjs__mod_os_init(ctx, ns);
   191	    tjs__mod_process_init(ctx, ns);
   192	    tjs__mod_signals_init(ctx, ns);
   193	    tjs__mod_sqlite3_init(ctx, ns);
   194	    tjs__mod_streams_init(ctx, ns);
   195	    tjs__mod_tls_init(ctx, ns);
   196	    tjs__mod_sys_init(ctx, ns);
   197	    tjs__mod_text_coding_init(ctx, ns);
   198	    tjs__mod_timers_init(ctx, ns);
   199	    tjs__mod_udp_init(ctx, ns);
   200	    tjs__mod_url_init(ctx, ns);
   201	    tjs__mod_wasm_init(ctx, ns);
   202	    tjs__mod_worker_init(ctx, ns);
   203	    tjs__mod_hashing_init(ctx, ns);
   204	    tjs__mod_httpclient_init(ctx, ns);
   205	    tjs__mod_miniz_init(ctx, ns);
   206	    tjs__webcrypto_init(ctx, ns);

   208	    tjs__mod_httpserver_init(ctx, ns);
   209	#ifndef _WIN32
   210	    tjs__mod_posix_socket_init(ctx, ns);
   211	#endif
   212	
   213	    /* Internal helpers. */
   214	    JS_DefinePropertyValueStr(ctx,
   215	                              ns,
   216	                              "drainMicrotasks",
   217	                              JS_NewCFunction(ctx, tjs__js_drain_microtasks, "drainMicrotasks", 0),
   218	                              JS_PROP_C_W_E);
   219	    JS_DefinePropertyValueStr(ctx,
   220	                              ns,
   221	                              "setCookieJarPath",
   222	                              JS_NewCFunction(ctx, tjs__set_cookie_jar_path, "setCookieJarPath", 1),
   223	                              JS_PROP_C_W_E);
   224	    JS_DefinePropertyValueStr(ctx,
   225	                              ns,
   226	                              "setCABundlePath",
   227	                              JS_NewCFunction(ctx, tjs__set_ca_bundle_path, "setCABundlePath", 1),
   228	                              JS_PROP_C_W_E);
   229	}

   231	JSValue tjs__get_args(JSContext *ctx) {
   232	    JSValue args = JS_NewArray(ctx);
   233	    for (int i = 0; i < tjs__argc; i++) {
   234	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(ctx, args, i, JS_NewString(ctx, tjs__argv[i]));
   235	    }
   236	    return args;
   237	}
   238	
   239	static JSValue tjs__dispatch_event(JSContext *ctx, JSValue *event) {
   240	    TJSRuntime *qrt = TJS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   241	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   242	
   243	    if (qrt->freeing) {
   244	        return JS_UNDEFINED;
   245	    }
   246	
   247	    JSValue global_obj = JS_GetGlobalObject(ctx);
   248	    JSValue ret = JS_Call(ctx, qrt->builtins.dispatch_event_func, global_obj, 1, event);
   249	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, global_obj);
   250	
   251	    return ret;
   252	}
   253	
   254	static void tjs__pending_rejections_add(TJSRuntime *qrt, JSContext *ctx, JSValue promise, JSValue reason) {
   255	    TJSPendingRejection *pr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*pr));
   256	    if (!pr) {
   257	        return;
   258	    }
   259	    pr->promise = JS_DupValue(ctx, promise);
   260	    pr->reason = JS_DupValue(ctx, reason);
   261	    list_add_tail(&pr->link, &qrt->pending_rejections);
   262	}
   263	
   264	static void tjs__pending_rejections_remove(TJSRuntime *qrt, JSContext *ctx, JSValue promise) {
   265	    struct list_head *el, *el1;
   266	    list_for_each_safe(el, el1, &qrt->pending_rejections) {
   267	        TJSPendingRejection *pr = list_entry(el, TJSPendingRejection, link);
   268	        if (JS_VALUE_GET_PTR(pr->promise) == JS_VALUE_GET_PTR(promise)) {
   269	            JS_FreeValue(ctx, pr->promise);
   270	            JS_FreeValue(ctx, pr->reason);
   271	            list_del(&pr->link);
   272	            js_free(ctx, pr);
   273	            return;
   274	        }
   275	    }
   276	}
   277	
   278	static void tjs__promise_rejection_tracker(JSContext *ctx,
   279	                                           JSValue promise,
   280	                                           JSValue reason,
   281	                                           bool is_handled,
   282	                                           void *opaque) {
   283	    TJSRuntime *qrt = TJS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   284	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   285	
   286	    if (qrt->freeing) {
   287	        return;
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    if (!is_handled) {
   291	        /* Defer event dispatch: the promise may get a handler attached
   292	         * synchronously (e.g. Promise.reject(x).catch(fn)) before the
   293	         * current microtask batch completes. Record the rejection and
   294	         * process it after all pending jobs have been executed, matching
   295	         * browser/Node.js behavior. */
   296	        tjs__pending_rejections_add(qrt, ctx, promise, reason);
   297	    } else {
   298	        /* The rejection is now handled (e.g. via .catch() or await in
   299	         * try/catch). Remove it from the pending list so no event fires. */
   300	        tjs__pending_rejections_remove(qrt, ctx, promise);
   301	    }
   302	}
   303	
   304	static void uv__stop(uv_async_t *handle) {
   305	    TJSRuntime *qrt = handle->data;
   306	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(qrt);
   307	
   308	    uv_stop(&qrt->loop);
   309	}

   311	void TJS_DefaultOptions(TJSRunOptions *options) {
   312	    static TJSRunOptions default_options = { .mem_limit = 0, .stack_size = TJS__DEFAULT_STACK_SIZE };
   313	
   314	    memcpy(options, &default_options, sizeof(*options));
   315	}
   316	
   317	TJSRuntime *TJS_NewRuntime(void) {

   320	    return TJS_NewRuntimeInternal(false, &options);
   321	}

   324	    return TJS_NewRuntimeInternal(false, options);
   325	}
   326	
   327	TJSRuntime *TJS_NewRuntimeWorker(void) {
   328	    TJSRunOptions options;
   329	    TJS_DefaultOptions(&options);
   330	    return TJS_NewRuntimeInternal(true, &options);
   331	}
   332	
   333	TJSRuntime *TJS_NewRuntimeInternal(bool is_worker, TJSRunOptions *options) {
   334	    JSRuntime *rt = NULL;
   335	    JSContext *ctx = NULL;
   336	    TJSRuntime *qrt = tjs__mallocz(sizeof(*qrt));
   337	
   338	    memcpy(&qrt->options, options, sizeof(*options));
   339	
   340	    rt = JS_NewRuntime2(&tjs_mf, NULL);
   341	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(rt);
   342	    qrt->rt = rt;
   343	
   344	#ifndef NDEBUG
   345	    JS_SetDumpFlags(rt, JS_DUMP_LEAKS);
   346	#endif
   347	
   348	    ctx = JS_NewContext(rt);
   349	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(ctx);
   350	    qrt->ctx = ctx;
   351	
   352	    JS_SetRuntimeOpaque(rt, qrt);
   353	    JS_SetContextOpaque(ctx, qrt);
   354	
   355	    /* Set memory limit */
   356	    JS_SetMemoryLimit(rt, options->mem_limit);
   357	
   358	    /* Set stack size */
   359	    JS_SetMaxStackSize(rt, options->stack_size);
   360	
   361	    /* SharedArrayBuffer functions */
   362	    JS_SetSharedArrayBufferFunctions(rt, &tjs_sf);
   363	
   364	    /* Worker support */
   365	    qrt->is_worker = is_worker;
   366	    JS_SetCanBlock(rt, is_worker);
   367	
   368	    CHECK_EQ(uv_loop_init(&qrt->loop), 0);
   369	
   370	    /* handle which runs the job queue */
   371	    CHECK_EQ(uv_prepare_init(&qrt->loop, &qrt->jobs.prepare), 0);
   372	    qrt->jobs.prepare.data = qrt;
   373	
   374	    /* handle to prevent the loop from blocking for i/o when there are pending jobs. */
   375	    CHECK_EQ(uv_idle_init(&qrt->loop, &qrt->jobs.idle), 0);
   376	    qrt->jobs.idle.data = qrt;
   377	
   378	    /* handle which runs the job queue */
   379	    CHECK_EQ(uv_check_init(&qrt->loop, &qrt->jobs.check), 0);
   380	    qrt->jobs.check.data = qrt;
   381	
   382	    /* handle for stopping this runtime (also works from another thread) */
   383	    CHECK_EQ(uv_async_init(&qrt->loop, &qrt->stop, uv__stop), 0);
   384	    qrt->stop.data = qrt;
   385	
   386	    /* loader for ES modules */
   387	    JS_SetModuleLoaderFunc2(rt, tjs_module_normalizer, tjs_module_loader, tjs_module_attr_checker, qrt);
   388	
   389	    /* unhandled promise rejection tracker */
   390	    JS_SetHostPromiseRejectionTracker(rt, tjs__promise_rejection_tracker, NULL);
   391	
   392	    /* start bootstrap */
   393	    JSValue global_obj = JS_GetGlobalObject(ctx);
   394	    JSValue core_sym = JS_NewSymbol(ctx, "tjs.internal.core", true);
   395	    JSAtom core_atom = JS_ValueToAtom(ctx, core_sym);
   396	    JSValue core = JS_NewObjectProto(ctx, JS_NULL);
   397	
   398	    CHECK_EQ(JS_DefinePropertyValue(ctx, global_obj, core_atom, core, JS_PROP_C_W_E), true);
   399	    CHECK_EQ(JS_DefinePropertyValueStr(ctx, core, "isWorker", JS_NewBool(ctx, is_worker), JS_PROP_C_W_E), true);
   400	
   401	    tjs__bootstrap_core(ctx, core);
   402	
   403	    CHECK_EQ(tjs__eval_bytecode(ctx, tjs__polyfills, tjs__polyfills_size, true), 0);
   404	    CHECK_EQ(tjs__eval_bytecode(ctx, tjs__core, tjs__core_size, true), 0);
   405	
   406	    /* Load some builtin references for easy access */
   407	    qrt->builtins.dispatch_event_func = JS_GetPropertyStr(ctx, global_obj, "dispatchEvent");
   408	    CHECK_EQ(JS_IsUndefined(qrt->builtins.dispatch_event_func), 0);
   409	    qrt->builtins.promise_event_ctor = JS_GetPropertyStr(qrt->ctx, global_obj, "PromiseRejectionEvent");
   410	    CHECK_EQ(JS_IsUndefined(qrt->builtins.promise_event_ctor), 0);
   411	
   412	    /* end bootstrap */
   413	    JS_FreeAtom(ctx, core_atom);
   414	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, core_sym);
   415	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, global_obj);
   416	
   417	    /* WASM */
   418	    RuntimeInitArgs wasm_init_args;
   419	    memset(&wasm_init_args, 0, sizeof(wasm_init_args));
   420	    wasm_init_args.mem_alloc_type = Alloc_With_Allocator;
   421	    wasm_init_args.mem_alloc_option.allocator.malloc_func = tjs__malloc;
   422	    wasm_init_args.mem_alloc_option.allocator.realloc_func = tjs__realloc;
   423	    wasm_init_args.mem_alloc_option.allocator.free_func = tjs__free;
   424	    CHECK_EQ(wasm_runtime_full_init(&wasm_init_args), true);
   425	    qrt->wasm_ctx.initialized = true;
   426	    qrt->wasm_ctx.stack_size = 512 * 1024;
   427	
   428	    /* Timers */
   429	    qrt->timers.timers = NULL;
   430	    qrt->timers.next_timer = 1;
   431	
   432	    /* Pending rejection tracking */
   433	    init_list_head(&qrt->pending_rejections);
   434	
   435	    return qrt;
   436	}
   437	
   438	void TJS_FreeRuntime(TJSRuntime *qrt) {
   439	    qrt->freeing = true;
   440	
   441	    /* Close all core loop handles. */
   442	    uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &qrt->jobs.prepare, NULL);
   443	    uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &qrt->jobs.idle, NULL);
   444	    uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &qrt->jobs.check, NULL);
   445	    uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &qrt->stop, NULL);
   446	
   447	    /* Destroy all timers */
   448	    tjs__destroy_timers(qrt);
   449	
   450	    /* Destroy lws context. Must happen before freeing the JS engine
   451	     * so that any remaining WSI_DESTROY callbacks can release GC refs. */
   452	    if (qrt->lws.ctx) {
   453	        lws_context_destroy(qrt->lws.ctx);
   454	        qrt->lws.ctx = NULL;
   455	        uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &qrt->lws.keepalive, NULL);
   456	    }
   457	
   458	    for (int i = 0; i < qrt->lws.no_proxy_count; i++) {
   459	        js_free(qrt->ctx, qrt->lws.no_proxy_entries[i]);
   460	    }
   461	    js_free(qrt->ctx, qrt->lws.no_proxy_entries);
   462	    qrt->lws.no_proxy_entries = NULL;
   463	    qrt->lws.no_proxy_count = 0;
   464	
   465	    js_free(qrt->ctx, qrt->lws.cookie_jar_path);
   466	    qrt->lws.cookie_jar_path = NULL;
   467	    js_free(qrt->ctx, qrt->lws.ca_bundle_path);
   468	    qrt->lws.ca_bundle_path = NULL;
   469	    js_free(qrt->ctx, qrt->lws.ca_bundle_data);
   470	    qrt->lws.ca_bundle_data = NULL;
   471	
   472	    /* Destroy shared TLS context. */
   473	    tjs__mod_tls_cleanup(qrt);
   474	
   475	    /* Destroy the JS engine. */
   476	    JS_FreeValue(qrt->ctx, qrt->builtins.dispatch_event_func);
   477	    qrt->builtins.dispatch_event_func = JS_UNDEFINED;
   478	    JS_FreeValue(qrt->ctx, qrt->builtins.promise_event_ctor);
   479	    qrt->builtins.promise_event_ctor = JS_UNDEFINED;
   480	    {
   481	        struct list_head *el, *el1;
   482	        list_for_each_safe(el, el1, &qrt->pending_rejections) {
   483	            TJSPendingRejection *pr = list_entry(el, TJSPendingRejection, link);
   484	            JS_FreeValue(qrt->ctx, pr->promise);
   485	            JS_FreeValue(qrt->ctx, pr->reason);
   486	            list_del(&pr->link);
   487	            js_free(qrt->ctx, pr);
   488	        }
   489	    }
   490	    JS_FreeContext(qrt->ctx);
   491	    JS_FreeRuntime(qrt->rt);
   492	
   493	    /* Destroy WASM runtime. */
   494	    if (qrt->wasm_ctx.initialized) {
   495	        wasm_runtime_destroy();
   496	        qrt->wasm_ctx.initialized = false;
   497	    }
   498

Now I can see the key issue. Let me look at the `HttpServer`'s `this_val` field. Notice that in the `TJSHttpServer` struct (line 124 of httpserver.c), there's a `JSValue this_val;` field that says `/* prevent GC while listening */`. This is the mechanism that keeps the server alive and prevents GC from collecting it.

Now let's look at the `TJSFsWatch` struct in `mod_fswatch.c`:

```c
typedef struct {
    JSContext *ctx;
    uv_fs_event_t handle;
    JSValue callback;
    int closed;
    int finalized;
} TJSFsWatch;
```

It does NOT have a `this_val` field. This means the JS object can be garbage collected while the native handle is still active. When the JS object is GC'd, the finalizer is called, which closes the handle. But the issue is that the `FileWatcher` should keep the process running and only be cleaned up when `FW.close()` is called.

The key difference is: in `TJSHttpServer`, the `this_val` stores a reference to the JS object, which prevents GC. The FileWatcher should do the same.

But wait, let me re-read the PR description more carefully:

> The `FileWatcher` will stop working if the FileWatcher object is collected by GC, it should keep process running and only be cleaned up when `FW.close()` is called, just like `tjs.serve`.

So the issue is that if you don't keep a reference to the FileWatcher object in JS, it gets garbage collected and stops working. The fix should be similar to how `tjs.serve` handles it - by storing a reference to the JS object (`this_val`) in the native struct to prevent GC.

Let me look at how `TJSHttpServer` uses `this_val`

   208	static void tjs_httpserver_finalizer(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val) {
   209	    TJSHttpServer *s = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_httpserver_class_id);
   210	    if (s) {
   211	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->callback);
   212	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->body_chunk_callback);
   213	
   214	        for (int i = 0; i < WS_EVENT_MAX; i++) {
   215	            JS_FreeValueRT(rt, s->ws_callbacks[i]);
   216	        }
   217	
   218	        TJSHttpRequest *req, *tmp;
   219	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->active_requests, req, tmp) {
   220	            HASH_DEL(s->active_requests, req);
   221	            tjs_http_req_free(rt, req);
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        /* Release any unconsumed upgrade contexts. */
   225	        TJSUpgradeCtx *uctx, *uctx_tmp;
   226	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->upgrade_contexts, uctx, uctx_tmp) {
   227	            HASH_DEL(s->upgrade_contexts, uctx);
   228	            js_free_rt(rt, uctx);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        /* Release any pending WS upgrades that never completed. */
   232	        TJSWsConnection *ws, *ws_tmp;
   233	        HASH_ITER(hh, s->pending_upgrades, ws, ws_tmp) {
   234	            HASH_DEL(s->pending_upgrades, ws);
   235	            JSValue cls_val = ws->this_val;
   236	            ws->this_val = JS_UNDEFINED;
   237	            JS_FreeValueRT(rt, cls_val);
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_cert_mem);
   241	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_key_mem);
   242	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_ca_mem);
   243	        js_free_rt(rt, s->ssl_passphrase);
   244	
   245	        js_free_rt(rt, s);
   246	    }
   247	}

   249	static void tjs_httpserver_mark(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val, JS_MarkFunc *mark_func) {
   250	    TJSHttpServer *s = JS_GetOpaque(val, tjs_httpserver_class_id);
   251	    if (s) {
   252	        JS_MarkValue(rt, s->callback, mark_func);

   277	static void tjs_http_custom_header_cb(const char *name, int nlen, void *opaque) {
   278	    TJSHeaderCollectCtx *hctx = (TJSHeaderCollectCtx *) opaque;
   279	
   280	    int total_len = lws_hdr_custom_length(hctx->wsi, name, nlen);
   281	    if (total_len < 0) {
   282	        return;
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    size_t buf_size = (size_t) total_len + 1;
   286	    char *val = js_malloc(hctx->ctx, buf_size);
   287	    if (!val) {
   288	        return;
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    int vlen = lws_hdr_custom_copy(hctx->wsi, val, (int) buf_size, name, nlen);
   292	    if (vlen >= 0) {
   293	        /* name includes trailing ':', strip it. */
   294	        int name_len = nlen;
   295	        if (name_len > 0 && name[name_len - 1] == ':') {
   296	            name_len--;
   297	        }
   298	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(hctx->ctx, hctx->arr, hctx->idx++, JS_NewStringLen(hctx->ctx, name, name_len));
   299	        JS_SetPropertyUint32(hctx->ctx, hctx->arr, hctx->idx++, JS_NewStringLen(hctx->ctx, val, vlen));
   300	    }

     5	const CHUNK_SIZE = 16640;
     6	
     7	const kReadable = Symbol('kReadable');
     8	const kWritable = Symbol('kWritable');
     9	
    10	const fhProxyHandler = {
    11	    get (target, prop) {
    12	        switch (prop) {
    13	            case 'readable': {
    14	                if (!target[kReadable]) {
    15	                    target[kReadable] = new ReadableStream({
    16	                        autoAllocateChunkSize: CHUNK_SIZE,
    17	                        type: 'bytes',
    18	                        async pull(controller) {
    19	                            const buf = controller.byobRequest.view;
    20	
    21	                            try {
    22	                                const nread = await target.read(buf);
    23	
    24	                                if (nread === null) {
    25	                                    controller.close();
    26	                                    controller.byobRequest.respond(0);
    27	                                } else {
    28	                                    controller.byobRequest.respond(nread);
    29	                                }
    30	                            } catch (e) {
    31	                                controller.error(e);
    32	                            }
    33	                        }
    34	                    });
    35	                }
    36	
    37	                return target[kReadable];
    38	            }
    39	
    40	            case 'writable': {
    41	                if (!target[kWritable]) {
    42	                    target[kWritable] = new WritableStream({
    43	                        async write(chunk) {
    44	                            await target.write(chunk);
    45	                        },
    46	                        async close() {
    47	                            await target.close();
    48	                        },
    49	                        async abort() {
    50	                            await target.close();
    51	                        }
    52	                    });
    53	                }
    54	
    55	                return target[kWritable];
    56	            }
    57	
    58	            default: {
    59	                if (typeof target[prop] === 'function') {
    60	                    return (...args) => target[prop].apply(target, args);
    61	                }
    62	
    63	                return target[prop];
    64	            }
    65	        }
    66	    }
    67	};

    81	export async function makeDir(path, options = { mode: 0o777, recursive: false }) {
    82	    if (!options.recursive) {
    83	        return core.mkdir(path, options.mode);
    84	    }
    85	
    86	    const parent = pathModule.dirname(path);
    87	
    88	    if (parent === path) {
    89	        return;
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    await makeDir(parent, options);
    93	
    94	    try {
    95	        return await core.mkdir(path, options.mode);
    96	    } catch (e) {
    97	        // Cannot rely on checking for EEXIST since the OS could throw other errors like EROFS.
    98	
    99	        const st = await core.stat(path);
   100	
   101	        if (!st.isDirectory) {
   102	            throw e;
   103	        }

   107	export async function symlink(path, newPath, options) {
   108	    const type = options?.type ?? 'file';
   109	    let flags = 0;
   110	
   111	    if (type === 'directory') {
   112	        flags = core.FS_SYMLINK_DIR;
   113	    } else if (type === 'junction') {
   114	        flags = core.FS_SYMLINK_JUNCTION;
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    return core.symlink(path, newPath, flags);
   118	}

   120	export async function writeFile(path, data, options = {}) {
   121	    const mode = options.mode ?? 0o644;
   122	    const f = await core.open(path, 'w', mode);
   123	
   124	    try {
   125	        if (typeof data === 'string') {
   126	            data = new TextEncoder().encode(data);
   127	        }
   128	
   129	        await f.write(data);
   130	    } finally {
   131	        await f.close();
   132	    }
   133	}

   135	// This is an adaptation of the 'rimraf' version bundled in Node.
   136	//
   137	
   138	const notEmptyErrors = new Set([
   139	    'ENOTEMPTY',
   140	    'EEXIST',
   141	    'EPERM'
   142	]);
   143	const retryErrors = new Set([
   144	    'EBUSY',
   145	    'EMFILE',
   146	    'ENFILE',
   147	    'ENOTEMPTY',
   148	    'EPERM'
   149	]);
   150	const isWindows = core.platform === 'windows';
   151	const _epermHandler = isWindows ? _fixWinEPERM : _rmdir;
   152	
   153	export async function remove(path, options = {}) {
   154	    options = { maxRetries: 0, retryDelay: 100, ...options };
   155	    let stats;
   156	
   157	    try {
   158	        stats = await core.lstat(path);
   159	    } catch (err) {
   160	        if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   161	            return;
   162	        }
   163	
   164	        // Windows can EPERM on stat.
   165	        if (isWindows && err.code === 'EPERM') {
   166	            await _fixWinEPERM(path, options, err);
   167	        }
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    try {
   171	        if (stats?.isDirectory) {
   172	            await _rmdir(path, options, null);
   173	        } else {
   174	            await _unlink(path, options);
   175	        }
   176	    } catch (err) {
   177	        if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   178	            return;
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        if (err.code === 'EPERM') {
   182	            return _epermHandler(path, options, err);
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (err.code !== 'EISDIR') {
   186	            throw err;
   187	        }
   188	
   189	        await _rmdir(path, options, err);
   190	    }
   191	}
   192	
   193	
   194	async function _unlink(path, options) {
   195	    const tries = options.maxRetries + 1;
   196	
   197	    for (let i = 1; i <= tries; i++) {
   198	        try {
   199	            return core.unlink(path);
   200	        } catch (err) {
   201	            // Only sleep if this is not the last try, and the delay is greater
   202	            // than zero, and an error was encountered that warrants a retry.
   203	            if (retryErrors.has(err.code) && i < tries && options.retryDelay > 0) {
   204	                await sleep(i * options.retryDelay);
   205	            } else if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   206	                // The file is already gone.
   207	                return;
   208	            } else if (i === tries) {
   209	                throw err;
   210	            }
   211	        }
   212	    }
   213	}
   214	
   215	
   216	async function _rmdir(path, options, originalErr) {
   217	    try {
   218	        await core.rmdir(path);
   219	    } catch (err) {
   220	        if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   221	            return;
   222	        }
   223	
   224	        if (err.code === 'ENOTDIR') {
   225	            throw originalErr || err;
   226	        }
   227	
   228	        if (notEmptyErrors.has(err.code)) {
   229	            // Removing failed. Try removing all children and then retrying the
   230	            // original removal. Windows has a habit of not closing handles promptly
   231	            // when files are deleted, resulting in spurious ENOTEMPTY failures. Work
   232	            // around that issue by retrying on Windows.
   233	
   234	            const dirIter = await core.readDir(path);
   235	
   236	            for await (const item of dirIter) {
   237	                const childPath = pathModule.join(path, item.name);
   238	
   239	                await remove(childPath, options);
   240	            }
   241	
   242	            const tries = options.maxRetries + 1;
   243	
   244	            for (let i = 1; i <= tries; i++) {
   245	                try {
   246	                    return core.rmdir(path);
   247	                } catch (err) {
   248	                    // Only sleep if this is not the last try, and the delay is greater
   249	                    // than zero, and an error was encountered that warrants a retry.
   250	                    if (retryErrors.has(err.code) && i < tries && options.retryDelay > 0) {
   251	                        await sleep(i * options.retryDelay);
   252	                    } else if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   253	                        // The file is already gone.
   254	                        return;
   255	                    } else if (i === tries) {
   256	                        throw err;
   257	                    }
   258	                }
   259	            }
   260	        }
   261	
   262	        throw originalErr || err;
   263	    }
   264	}
   265	
   266	
   267	async function _fixWinEPERM(path, options, originalErr) {
   268	    try {
   269	        await core.chmod(path, 0o666);
   270	    } catch (err) {
   271	        if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   272	            return;
   273	        }
   274	
   275	        throw originalErr;
   276	    }
   277	
   278	    let stats;
   279	
   280	    try {
   281	        stats = await core.stat(path);
   282	    } catch (err) {
   283	        if (err.code === 'ENOENT') {
   284	            return;
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        throw originalErr;
   288	    }
   289	
   290	    if (stats.isDirectory) {
   291	        return _rmdir(path, options, originalErr);
   292	    } else {
   293	        return _unlink(path, options);
   294	    }
   295	}
   296	
   297	async function sleep(ms) {
   298	    return new Promise(resolve => {
   299	        setTimeout(resolve, ms);
   300	    });
   301	}

2026-05-28 17:52:30,127 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear understanding. The issue is in `mod_fswatch.c`. The `TJSFsWatch` struct doesn't keep a reference to the JS object (`this_val`), so when the JS user doesn't hold a reference to the FileWatcher object, it gets garbage collected, which triggers the finalizer and closes the watch.

The fix is to add a `this_val` field to `TJSFsWatch` similar to what `TJSHttpServer` has. This way, the native code holds a reference to the JS object, preventing GC. Then, when `close()` is explicitly called, we release that reference.

Let me now write a reproduction script first

🎬 ACTION
cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_fswatch_gc.js << 'EOF'
// Test to reproduce the FileWatcher GC issue
// If the FileWatcher object is GC'd, it stops working.

const tmpDir = tjs.makeTempDir('test_fswatch_gcXXXXXX');
const filePath = tmpDir + '/test.txt';

// Create initial file
const f = tjs.makeTempFile(filePath);
f.close();

let eventCount = 0;

// This one should work - we keep a reference
const watcher1 = tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher1:', event, path);
});

// This one should also work even without holding the reference
// According to the PR, it should NOT be GC'd
tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher2 (no ref):', event, path);
});

// Force GC if possible
if (typeof Bun !== 'undefined' && Bun.gc) {
    Bun.gc(true);
}

// Sleep to let file system events settle
setTimeout(() => {
    // Trigger a change
    const f2 = tjs.open(filePath, 'w');
    f2.write(new TextEncoder().encode('hello'));
    f2.close();
    console.log('Wrote to file');
}, 500);

setTimeout(() => {
    console.log('Total events:', eventCount);
    // Both watchers should have fired
    if (eventCount >= 2) {
        console.log('SUCCESS: Both watchers working');
    } else {
        console.log('FAIL: Not enough events (GC issue?)');
    }
    watcher1.close();
    tjs.remove(tmpDir);
}, 2000);
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_fswatch_gc.js << 'EOF'
// Test to reproduce the FileWatcher GC issue
import * as tjs from 'tjs';

const tmpDir = tjs.makeTempDir('test_fswatch_gcXXXXXX');

let eventCount = 0;

// This one should work - we keep a reference
const watcher1 = tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher1:', event, path);
});

// This one should also work even without holding the reference
// According to the PR, it should NOT be GC'd
tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher2 (no ref):', event, path);
});

// Sleep to let file system events settle
setTimeout(() => {
    // Trigger a change by creating a file
    const f = tjs.makeTempFile(tmpDir + '/test_fileXXXXXX');
    const p = f.path;
    f.write(new TextEncoder().encode('hello'));
    f.close();
    console.log('Wrote to file:', p);
}, 500);

setTimeout(() => {
    console.log('Total events:', eventCount);
    // Both watchers should have fired
    if (eventCount >= 2) {
        console.log('SUCCESS: Both watchers working');
    } else {
        console.log('FAIL: Not enough events (GC issue?)');
    }
    watcher1.close();
    tjs.remove(tmpDir);
}, 3000);
EOF

cd /testbed && cat > /tmp/test_fswatch_gc.js << 'EOF'
// Test to reproduce the FileWatcher GC issue

const encoder = new TextEncoder();

let eventCount = 0;

const tmpDir = tjs.makeTempDir('test_fswatch_gcXXXXXX');

// This one should work - we keep a reference
const watcher1 = tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher1:', event, path);
});

// This one should also work even without holding the reference
// According to the PR, it should NOT be GC'd
tjs.watch(tmpDir, (path, event) => {
    eventCount++;
    console.log('watcher2 (no ref):', event, path);
});

async function sleep(ms) {
    return new Promise(resolve => {
        setTimeout(resolve, ms);
    });
}

async function main() {
    await sleep(500);
    // Trigger a change by creating a file
    const f = tjs.makeTempFile(tmpDir + '/test_fileXXXXXX');
    const p = f.path;
    console.log('Writing to:', p);
    await f.write(encoder.encode('hello'));
    await f.close();
    console.log('Wrote to file');

    await sleep(1000);
    console.log('Total events:', eventCount);
    // Both watchers should have fired
    if (eventCount >= 2) {
        console.log('SUCCESS: Both watchers working');
    } else {
        console.log('FAIL: Not enough events (GC issue?)');
    }
    watcher1.close();
    await tjs.remove(tmpDir);
}

main();
EOF

static JSValue tjs_fs_mkdtemp(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *tpl = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!tpl) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, tpl);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_mkdtemp(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, tpl, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, tpl);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static JSValue tjs_fsreq_init(JSContext *ctx, TJSFsReq *fr, JSValue obj) {
    fr->ctx = ctx;
    fr->req.data = fr;
    fr->obj = JS_DupValue(ctx, obj);
    tjs_buf_ref_init(&fr->buf_ref);

    return TJS_InitPromise(ctx, &fr->result);
}

static void uv__fs_req_cb(uv_fs_t *req) {
    TJSFsReq *fr = req->data;
    if (!fr) {
        return;
    }

    JSContext *ctx = fr->ctx;
    JSValue arg;
    TJSFile *f;
    TJSDir *d;
    bool is_reject = false;

    if (req->result < 0) {
        arg = tjs_new_error(ctx, fr->req.result);
        is_reject = true;
        goto skip;
    }

    switch (req->fs_type) {
        case UV_FS_OPEN:
            arg = tjs_new_file(ctx, fr->req.result, fr->req.path);
            break;
--
    tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
    fr->buf_ref = buf_ref;
    return fr->result.p;
}

static JSValue tjs_file_close(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_close(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, f->fd, uv__fs_req_cb);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
}

}

static JSValue tjs_file_truncate(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int64_t offset = 0;
    if (!JS_IsUndefined(argv[0]) && JS_ToInt64(ctx, &offset, argv[0])) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_ftruncate(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, f->fd, offset, uv__fs_req_cb);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
}

}

static JSValue tjs_file_chmod(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int mode;
    if (JS_IsUndefined(argv[0]) || JS_ToInt32(ctx, &mode, argv[0])) {
        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "expected a number for mode parameter");
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_fchmod(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, f->fd, mode, uv__fs_req_cb);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
}

static JSValue tjs_file_chown(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int uid;
    if (JS_IsUndefined(argv[0]) || JS_ToInt32(ctx, &uid, argv[0])) {
        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "expected a number for uid parameter");
    }

    int gid;
    if (JS_IsUndefined(argv[1]) || JS_ToInt32(ctx, &gid, argv[1])) {
        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "expected a number for gid parameter");
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_fchown(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, f->fd, uid, gid, uv__fs_req_cb);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
}

static JSValue tjs_file_utime(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    double atime;
    if (JS_ToFloat64(ctx, &atime, argv[0])) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    double mtime;
    if (JS_ToFloat64(ctx, &mtime, argv[1])) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    /* Date.getTime is in ms, convert to seconds. */
    int r = uv_fs_futime(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, f->fd, atime / 1000, mtime / 1000, uv__fs_req_cb);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, this_val);
}

static JSValue tjs_file_fileno(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    TJSFile *f = tjs_file_get(ctx, this_val);
    if (!f) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    return JS_NewInt32(ctx, f->fd);
}

static JSValue tjs_file_constructor(JSContext *ctx, JSValue new_target, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    uv_file fd;

    if (JS_ToInt32(ctx, &fd, argv[0])) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    const char *path = "";
    if (argc > 1 && JS_IsString(argv[1])) {
        path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[1]);
        if (!path) {
            return JS_EXCEPTION;
        }
    }

    JSValue obj = tjs_new_file(ctx, fd, path);

    if (argc > 1 && JS_IsString(argv[1])) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    }

    return obj;
}

    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
--
    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_stat_sync(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    uv_fs_t req;
    int r = uv_fs_stat(NULL, &req, path, NULL);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    if (r != 0) {
        uv_fs_req_cleanup(&req);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    JSValue ret = tjs_new_stat(ctx, &req.statbuf);
    uv_fs_req_cleanup(&req);

    return ret;
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_unlink(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_unlink(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, path, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_rename(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    const char *new_path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[1]);
    if (!new_path) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, new_path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_rename(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, path, new_path, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, new_path);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_mkdir(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int32_t mode = 0777;
    if (argc >= 2 && !JS_IsUndefined(argv[1])) {
        if (JS_ToInt32(ctx, &mode, argv[1])) {
            JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
            return JS_EXCEPTION;
        }
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_mkdir(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, path, mode, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static int tjs__mkdir_sync(const char *path, int mode) {
    uv_fs_t req;
    int r = uv_fs_mkdir(NULL, &req, path, mode, NULL);
    uv_fs_req_cleanup(&req);
    return r;
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_mkdir_sync(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int32_t mode = 0777;
    if (argc >= 2 && !JS_IsUndefined(argv[1])) {
        if (JS_ToInt32(ctx, &mode, argv[1])) {
            JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
            return JS_EXCEPTION;
        }
    }

    int r = tjs__mkdir_sync(path, mode);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    if (r != 0) {
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return JS_UNDEFINED;

}

static void tjs__readfile_work_cb(uv_work_t *req) {
    TJSReadFileReq *fr = req->data;
    CHECK_NOT_NULL(fr);

    fr->r = tjs__load_file(fr->ctx, &fr->dbuf, fr->filename);
}

static void tjs__readfile_after_work_cb(uv_work_t *req, int status) {
    TJSReadFileReq *fr = req->data;
    CHECK_NOT_NULL(fr);

    JSContext *ctx = fr->ctx;
    JSValue arg;
    bool is_reject = false;

    if (status != 0) {
        arg = tjs_new_error(ctx, status);
        is_reject = true;
    } else if (fr->r < 0) {
        arg = tjs_new_error(ctx, fr->r);
        is_reject = true;
    } else {
        /* The buffer was allocated with raw (untracked) realloc on the worker
           thread to avoid a data race on QJS malloc_state.  We must copy it
           into a QJS-tracked allocation here because ArrayBuffer.prototype.transfer
           calls js_realloc on the backing buffer, which would corrupt malloc_state
           if the buffer was never tracked. */
        size_t size = fr->dbuf.size;
--
    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

static JSValue tjs_fs_chmod(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    if (!JS_IsString(argv[0])) {
        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "expected a string for path parameter");
    }

    int mode;
    if (JS_IsUndefined(argv[1]) || JS_ToInt32(ctx, &mode, argv[1])) {
        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "expected a number for mode parameter");
    }

    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    TJSFsReq *fr = js_malloc(ctx, sizeof(*fr));
    if (!fr) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_chmod(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, path, mode, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
    if (r != 0) {
        js_free(ctx, fr);
        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
    }

    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

    if (!path) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    const char *path2 = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[1]);
    if (!path2) {
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path2);
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }

    int r = uv_fs_link(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fr->req, path, path2, uv__fs_req_cb);
    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
--
    return tjs_fsreq_init(ctx, fr, JS_UNDEFINED);
}

    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(this_val);
    if (!fw) {
        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    }
    if (!JS_IsUndefined(fw->this_val)) {
        JSValue val = fw->this_val;
        fw->this_val = JS_UNDEFINED;
        JS_FreeValue(ctx, val);
    }
    maybe_close(fw);
    return JS_UNDEFINED;
}'

    21	 * OUT OF OR IN CONNECTION WITH THE SOFTWARE OR THE USE OR OTHER DEALINGS IN
    22	 * THE SOFTWARE.
    23	 */
    24	
    25	#include "mem.h"
    26	#include "private.h"
    27	#include "utils.h"
    28	
    29	typedef struct {
    30	    JSContext *ctx;
    31	    uv_fs_event_t handle;
    32	    JSValue callback;
    33	    JSValue this_val;
    34	    int closed;
    35	    int finalized;
    36	} TJSFsWatch;
    37	
    38	static JSClassID tjs_fswatch_class_id;
    39	
    40	static TJSFsWatch *tjs_fswatch_get(JSValue obj) {
    41	    return JS_GetOpaque(obj, tjs_fswatch_class_id);
    42	}
    43	
    44	static void uv__fsevent_close_cb(uv_handle_t *handle) {
    45	    TJSFsWatch *fw = handle->data;
    46	    if (fw) {
    47	        fw->closed = 1;
    48	        if (fw->finalized) {
    49	            tjs__free(fw);
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	}
    53	
    54	static void maybe_close(TJSFsWatch *fw) {
    55	    if (!uv_is_closing((uv_handle_t *) &fw->handle)) {
    56	        uv_close((uv_handle_t *) &fw->handle, uv__fsevent_close_cb);
    57	    }
    58	}
    59	
    60	static void tjs_fswatch_finalizer(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val) {
    61	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(val);
    62	    if (fw) {
    63	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, fw->callback);
    64	        JS_FreeValueRT(rt, fw->this_val);
    65	        fw->this_val = JS_UNDEFINED;
    66	        fw->finalized = 1;
    67	        if (fw->closed) {
    68	            tjs__free(fw);
    69	        } else {
    70	            maybe_close(fw);
    71	        }
    72	    }
    73	}
    74	
    75	static void tjs_fswatch_mark(JSRuntime *rt, JSValue val, JS_MarkFunc *mark_func) {
    76	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(val);
    77	    if (fw) {
    78	        JS_MarkValue(rt, fw->callback, mark_func);
    79	        JS_MarkValue(rt, fw->this_val, mark_func);
    80	    }
    81	}
    82	
    83	static JSClassDef tjs_fswatch_class = {
    84	    "FsWatcher",
    85	    .finalizer = tjs_fswatch_finalizer,
    86	    .gc_mark = tjs_fswatch_mark,
    87	};
    88	
    89	static JSValue tjs_fswatch_close(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
    90	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(this_val);
    91	    if (!fw) {
    92	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
    93	    }
    94	    if (!JS_IsUndefined(fw->this_val)) {
    95	        JSValue val = fw->this_val;
    96	        fw->this_val = JS_UNDEFINED;
    97	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, val);
    98	    }
    99	    maybe_close(fw);
   100	    return JS_UNDEFINED;
   101	}
   102	
   103	static JSValue tjs_fswatch_path_get(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val) {
   104	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs_fswatch_get(this_val);
   105	    if (!fw) {
   106	        return JS_UNDEFINED;
   107	    }
   108	
   109	    char buf[1024];
   110	    size_t size = sizeof(buf);
   111	    char *dbuf = buf;
   112	    int r;
   113	
   114	    r = uv_fs_event_getpath(&fw->handle, dbuf, &size);
   115	    if (r != 0) {
   116	        if (r != UV_ENOBUFS) {
   117	            return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   118	        }
   119	        dbuf = js_malloc(ctx, size);
   120	        if (!dbuf) {
   121	            return JS_EXCEPTION;
   122	        }
   123	        uv_fs_event_getpath(&fw->handle, dbuf, &size);
   124	        if (r != 0) {
   125	            js_free(ctx, dbuf);
   126	            return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   127	        }
   128	    }
   129	
   130	    JSValue ret = JS_NewStringLen(ctx, dbuf, size);
   131	
   132	    if (dbuf != buf) {
   133	        js_free(ctx, dbuf);
   134	    }
   135	
   136	    return ret;
   137	}
   138	
   139	static void uv__fs_event_cb(uv_fs_event_t *handle, const char *filename, int events, int status) {
   140	    TJSFsWatch *fw = handle->data;
   141	    CHECK_NOT_NULL(fw);
   142	    JSContext *ctx = fw->ctx;
   143	
   144	    // TODO: handle error case?
   145	    if (status != 0) {
   146	        return;
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    // libuv could set both, if we get rename, ignore change.
   150	
   151	    JSValue event;
   152	    if (events & UV_RENAME) {
   153	        event = JS_NewString(ctx, "rename");
   154	    } else if (events & UV_CHANGE) {
   155	        event = JS_NewString(ctx, "change");
   156	    } else {
   157	        // This shouldn't happen.
   158	        CHECK(0 && "invalid fs events");
   159	        return;
   160	    }
   161	
   162	    JSValue args[2] = {
   163	        JS_NewString(ctx, filename),
   164	        event,
   165	    };
   166	
   167	    tjs_call_handler(ctx, fw->callback, countof(args), args);
   168	
   169	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, args[0]);
   170	    JS_FreeValue(ctx, args[1]);
   171	}
   172	
   173	static JSValue tjs_fs_watch(JSContext *ctx, JSValue this_val, int argc, JSValue *argv) {
   174	    const char *path = JS_ToCString(ctx, argv[0]);
   175	    if (!path) {
   176	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    if (!JS_IsFunction(ctx, argv[1])) {
   180	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   181	        return JS_ThrowTypeError(ctx, "no callback function provided");
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    JSValue obj = JS_NewObjectClass(ctx, tjs_fswatch_class_id);
   185	    if (JS_IsException(obj)) {
   186	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   187	        return JS_EXCEPTION;
   188	    }
   189	
   190	    TJSFsWatch *fw = tjs__mallocz(sizeof(*fw));
   191	    if (!fw) {
   192	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   193	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   194	        return JS_ThrowOutOfMemory(ctx);
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    int r = uv_fs_event_init(tjs_get_loop(ctx), &fw->handle);
   198	    if (r != 0) {
   199	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   200	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   201	        tjs__free(fw);
   202	        return JS_ThrowInternalError(ctx, "couldn't initialize handle");
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    r = uv_fs_event_start(&fw->handle, uv__fs_event_cb, path, UV_FS_EVENT_RECURSIVE);
   206	    if (r != 0) {
   207	        JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   208	        JS_FreeValue(ctx, obj);
   209	        tjs__free(fw);
   210	        return tjs_throw_errno(ctx, r);
   211	    }
   212	
   213	    JS_FreeCString(ctx, path);
   214	
   215	    fw->ctx = ctx;
   216	    fw->handle.data = fw;
   217	    fw->callback = JS_DupValue(ctx, argv[1]);
   218	    fw->this_val = JS_DupValue(ctx, obj);
   219	
   220	    JS_SetOpaque(obj, fw);
   221	    return obj;
   222	}
   223	
   224	static const JSCFunctionListEntry tjs_fswatch_proto_funcs[] = {
   225	    TJS_CFUNC_DEF("close", 0, tjs_fswatch_close),
   226	    JS_CGETSET_DEF("path", tjs_fswatch_path_get, NULL),
   227	    JS_PROP_STRING_DEF("[Symbol.toStringTag]", "FsWatcher", JS_PROP_CONFIGURABLE),
   228	};
   229	
   230	static const JSCFunctionListEntry tjs_fswatch_funcs[] = {
   231	    TJS_CFUNC_DEF("watch", 2, tjs_fs_watch),
   232	};
   233	
   234	void tjs__mod_fswatch_init(JSContext *ctx, JSValue ns) {
   235	    JSRuntime *rt = JS_GetRuntime(ctx);
   236	
   237	    JS_NewClassID(rt, &tjs_fswatch_class_id);
   238	    JS_NewClass(rt, tjs_fswatch_class_id, &tjs_fswatch_class);
   239	    JSValue proto = JS_NewObject(ctx);
   240	    JS_SetPropertyFunctionList(ctx, proto, tjs_fswatch_proto_funcs, countof(tjs_fswatch_proto_funcs));
   241	    JS_SetClassProto(ctx, tjs_fswatch_class_id, proto);
   242	
   243	    JS_SetPropertyFunctionList(ctx, ns, tjs_fswatch_funcs, countof(tjs_fswatch_funcs));
   244	}
   245

The existing test passes as well. Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **What if `close()` is called multiple times?** - The `maybe_close` function already checks `uv_is_closing`, so it won't double-close. And our `this_val` release checks `!JS_IsUndefined(fw->this_val)` before freeing, so it won't double-free.

2. **What if the watcher object is GC'd before `close()` is called?** - The finalizer will free both `callback` and `this_val`, then call `maybe_close` which closes the handle. This is correct.

3. **What if `close()` is called and then GC happens?** - `close()` clears `this_val` reference (allowing GC), then `maybe_close` starts the close process. When the handle closes, if the finalizer already ran (`finalized=1`), the memory is freed in `uv__fsevent_close_cb`. If the finalizer runs after close, it sees `closed=1` and frees immediately. The `this_val` is already cleared so no double-free.

4. **Memory leak check**: The `tjs__mallocz` call zero-initializes the struct, so `this_val` starts as `JS_UNDEFINED` (which is 0). After `JS_DupValue`, it holds a proper reference. Both `close()` and the finalizer properly release it.
